  <script>
   document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    if (wordpress.locale !== 'en_uk') {
      // Replace links to home page
      var homeLinksElems = document.querySelectorAll('a[href="https://www.nme.com/"]:not([hreflang])');
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(homeLinksElems, function(elem) {
        elem.href = 'https://www.nme.com/' + wordpress.locale + '/';
      });

      // Remove links that are not within the same language
      var homeLinksElems = document.querySelectorAll('.tdc-content-wrap a[href^="https://www.nme.com/"], .tdc-content-wrap a[href^="https://nme.com/"], .tdc-content-wrap a[href^="http://nme.com/"], .tdc-content-wrap a[href^="http://www.nme.com/"]');
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(homeLinksElems, function(elem) {
        if (elem.pathname.match(/^\/(wp-admin)/)) {
          return;
        }
        var regexp = new RegExp('^\\/(' + wordpress.locale + ')', 'g');
        if (!elem.pathname.match(regexp) && elem.closest('ul') && elem.closest('ul').innerHTML.match(/read more/i)) {
          elem.closest('ul').remove();
        } else if (!elem.pathname.match(regexp)) {
          elem.outerHTML = elem.innerHTML;
        }
      });
    }
  });
  </script>
  <script>
   document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    var listItems = document.querySelectorAll('.td-post-content ul');
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(listItems, function(elem) {
      if (elem.innerText.match(/^read more/gi)) {
        elem.classList.add('post-content-read-more');
        elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML.replace(/<(\/?)h[1-5]+>/g, '');
        elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML.replace(/read more(:?)/gi, '<span class="post-content-read-more-label">Read More:</span>');
      }
    });
  });
  </script>
  <script>
   function getJSON(url, successHandler, errorHandler) {
    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr.open('get', url, true);
    xhr.responseType = 'json';
    xhr.onload = function() {
      var status = xhr.status;
      if (status === 200) {
        return successHandler && successHandler(xhr.response);
      }
      return errorHandler && errorHandler(status);
    };
    xhr.send();
  }

  function getCountry() {
    if (td_read_site_cookie('country-name')) {
      return Promise.resolve(td_read_site_cookie('country-name'));
    }

    return new Promise(function(resolve) {
      getJSON('https://geo.bandlab.io/v2/ip/', function(data) {
        td_set_cookies_life(['country-name', data.countryName, 864E5 * 2]);
        resolve(data.countryName)
      });
    });
  }

  // Region restricted articles
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    var path = document.location.pathname;
    if (path.match(/(2558142|2558416|2583482|2574465|2579190|2558418)$/)) {
      document.body.style.display = 'none';
      getCountry().then(function(countryName) {
        if (countryName.indexOf('United Kingdom') === -1) {
          document.location.href = '/404';
          return;
        }
        document.body.style.display = 'block';
      });
    }
  });

  // Load trending block
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    var trendingBlocks = document.querySelectorAll('[data-trending]');

    if (!trendingBlocks.length) {
      return;
    }

    var pageId = 2588300;
    if (wordpress.locale === 'en_au') {
      pageId = 2609734;
    }

    getJSON(document.location.origin + '/wp-json/wp/v2/pages/' + pageId + '?lang=' + wordpress.locale + '&_fields=content.rendered,type,id', function(data) {
      try {
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(trendingBlocks, function(trendingBlock) {
          trendingBlock.innerHTML = jQuery(data.content.rendered).find('.td_flex_block')[0].outerHTML;

          var images = trendingBlock.querySelectorAll('[data-img-url]');
          Array.prototype.forEach.call(images, function(elem) {
            elem.style.backgroundImage = 'url(' + elem.getAttribute('data-img-url') + ')';
          });
        });
        window.dispatchEvent(new Event('resize'));
      } catch (e) {
        console.log(e);
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(trendingBlocks, function(elem) {
          elem.closest('.vc_raw_html').remove();
        });
      }
    });
  });

  // Load Film Custom block
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    var filmOutThisWeek = document.querySelectorAll('[film-out-this-week]');

    if (!filmOutThisWeek.length) {
      return;
    }

    var pageId = 2643047;
    if (wordpress.locale === 'en_au') {
      pageId = 2643047;
    }

    getJSON(document.location.origin + '/wp-json/wp/v2/pages/' + pageId + '?lang=' + wordpress.locale + '&_fields=content.rendered,type,id', function(data) {
      try {
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(filmOutThisWeek, function(customBlock) {
          customBlock.innerHTML = jQuery(data.content.rendered).find('.custom-block')[0].innerHTML;
        });
        window.dispatchEvent(new Event('resize'));
      } catch (e) {
        console.log(e);
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(filmOutThisWeek, function(elem) {
          elem.closest('.vc_raw_html').remove();
        });
      }
    });
  });

  // NME Asia Survey
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    if (wordpress.locale !== 'en_asia' || document.documentElement.clientWidth <= 1024) {
      return;
    }
    getCountry().then(function(countryName) {
      if (!countryName.match(/Singapore|Malaysia|Philippines/)) {
        return;
      }
      const elem = document.createElement('div');
      elem.className = 'survey-button-container';
      elem.innerHTML = '<a href="https://www.surveymonkey.com/r/WQHT72P" target="_blank" rel="nofollow" title="Participate to a quick survey">Feedback</a>';
      document.querySelector('body').appendChild(elem);
    });
  });
  </script>

             <script>
              (function() {
    let lang;
    switch (wordpress.locale) {
      case 'en_au':
        lang = 'en-au';
        break;
      case 'en_asia':
        lang = 'en-asia';
        break;
      default:
        lang = 'en-gb';
        break;
    }

    let category;

    if (wordpress && (wordpress.postCategories || wordpress.categories)) {
      const categories = wordpress.postCategories || wordpress.categories;

      if (categories.toString().toLowerCase().match(/(gaming|game-review)/g)) {
        category = 'gaming';
      } else if (categories.toString().toLowerCase().match(/(film|the-movies)/g)) {
        category = 'film';
      } else if (categories.toString().toLowerCase().match(/(tv)/g)) {
        category = 'tv';
      } else if (categories.toString().toLowerCase().match(/(music|album)/g)) {
        category = 'music';
      }
    } else if (wordpress && wordpress.pageId) {
      const film_pages = ['2661557', '2638248', '2723339'];
      const gaming_pages = ['2658361', '2638497', '2723337'];
      const music_pages = ['', '2649406', '2723320'];
      const news_pages = ['', '', ''];
      const tv_pages = ['', '2638199', '2723341'];
      if (gaming_pages.indexOf(wordpress.pageId) !== -1) {
        category = 'gaming';
      } else if (film_pages.indexOf(wordpress.pageId) !== -1) {
        category = 'film';
      } else if (music_pages.indexOf(wordpress.pageId) !== -1) {
        category = 'music';
      } else if (tv_pages.indexOf(wordpress.pageId) !== -1) {
        category = 'tv';
      }
    }

    if (category) {
      const navElement = document.querySelector('.category-nav-mobile-' + category);

      if (wordpress.locale !== 'en_uk') {
        navElement.querySelectorAll('a').forEach((elem) => {
          elem.href = elem.href.replace('nme.com/', 'nme.com/' + wordpress.locale + '/');
        });
      }
      if (navElement) {
        navElement.style.display = 'block';
      }

      document.querySelectorAll('.category-nav-mobile').forEach((elem) => {
        if (elem !== navElement) {
          elem.remove();
        }
      });
    } else {
      document.querySelector('.categories-navs-mobile').remove();
    }

    document.querySelectorAll('.categories-navs-mobile a').forEach((elem) => {
      elem.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (__gaTracker) {
          __gaTracker('send', 'event', 'Navigation', 'Sub Nav Mobile Click', elem.getAttribute('title'));
        }
      });
    });
  })();
             </script>
            </div>
           </div>

             <script>
              (function() {
    let lang;
    switch (wordpress.locale) {
      case 'en_au':
        lang = 'en-au';
        break;
      case 'en_asia':
        lang = 'en-asia';
        break;
      default:
        lang = 'en-gb';
        break;
    }

    if (['/', '/en_au/', '/en_asia/'].includes(document.location.pathname)) {
      const trendingBlockElem = document.querySelector('.category-nav-trending[lang="' + lang + '"]');
      if (trendingBlockElem) {
        trendingBlockElem.style.display = 'block';
        Array.from(trendingBlockElem.parentNode.children).forEach((child) => {
          if (child !== trendingBlockElem) {
            child.remove();
          }
        });
      } else {
        document.querySelector('.categories-navs').remove();
      }
      return;
    }

    let category;

    if (wordpress && (wordpress.postCategories || wordpress.categories)) {
      const categories = wordpress.postCategories || wordpress.categories;

      if (categories.toString().toLowerCase().match(/(gaming|game-review)/g)) {
        category = 'gaming';
      } else if (categories.toString().toLowerCase().match(/(film|the-movies)/g)) {
        category = 'film';
      } else if (categories.toString().toLowerCase().match(/(tv)/g)) {
        category = 'tv';
      } else if (categories.toString().toLowerCase().match(/(music|album)/g)) {
        category = 'music';
      }
    } else if (wordpress && wordpress.pageId) {
      const film_pages = ['2661557', '2638248', '2723339'];
      const gaming_pages = ['2658361', '2638497', '2723337'];
      const music_pages = ['', '2649406', '2723320'];
      const news_pages = ['', '', ''];
      const tv_pages = ['', '2638199', '2723341'];
      if (gaming_pages.indexOf(wordpress.pageId) !== -1) {
        category = 'gaming';
      } else if (film_pages.indexOf(wordpress.pageId) !== -1) {
        category = 'film';
      } else if (music_pages.indexOf(wordpress.pageId) !== -1) {
        category = 'music';
      } else if (tv_pages.indexOf(wordpress.pageId) !== -1) {
        category = 'tv';
      }
    }

    if (category) {
      const navElement = document.querySelector('.category-nav-' + category);

      if (wordpress.locale !== 'en_uk') {
        navElement.querySelectorAll('a').forEach((elem) => {
          elem.href = elem.href.replace('nme.com/', 'nme.com/' + wordpress.locale + '/');
        });
      }
      if (navElement) {
        navElement.style.display = 'block';
      }

      document.querySelectorAll('.category-nav').forEach((elem) => {
        if (elem !== navElement) {
          elem.remove();
        }
      });
    } else {
      document.querySelector('.categories-navs').remove();
    }

    document.querySelectorAll('.categories-navs a').forEach((elem) => {
      elem.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (__gaTracker) {
          __gaTracker('send', 'event', 'Navigation', 'Sub Nav Desktop Click', elem.getAttribute('title'));
        }
      });
    });
  })();
             </script>
            </div>

   googletag.cmd.push(function() {
    if (wordpress.hideAllAds) { return; }

    if (wordpress.pageId) {
      googletag.pubads().setTargeting('pageId', [wordpress.pageId]);
    } else if (wordpress.postId) {
      googletag.pubads().setTargeting('postId', [wordpress.postId]);
      if (wordpress.postCategories) {
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('category', wordpress.postCategories);
      }
    } else if (wordpress.categories) {
      googletag.pubads().setTargeting('category', wordpress.categories);
    }

    googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
    googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
    googletag.enableServices();
  });

   googletag.cmd.push(function() {
    if (wordpress.hideAllAds) { return; }

    var leaderboardMapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
      .addSize([1018, 0], [[728, 90], [970, 90], [970, 250]]) // Desktop
      .addSize([768, 0], [[320, 50], [728, 90]]) // Tablet
      .addSize([0, 0], [])
      .build();

    var sidebarMapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
      .addSize([1018, 0], [[300, 250], [300, 600]]) // Desktop
      .addSize([768, 0], []) // Tablet
      .addSize([0, 0], [300, 250])
      .build();

    var storyMapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
      .addSize([1018, 0], [[728, 90], [970, 90], [970, 250]]) // Desktop
      .addSize([768, 0], [[320, 50], [728, 90]]) // Tablet
      .addSize([0, 0], [[300, 250]])
      .build();

    window.amsSlots = [];

    if (document.documentElement.clientWidth >= 768) {
      var abTestLeaderboardPosition = Math.floor((Math.random() * 2));
      if (abTestLeaderboardPosition) {
        // document.querySelector('.td-header-desktop-wrap').classList.add('test-billboard-viewability');
      }
      // Leaderboard
      googletag
        .defineSlot('/21758830223/nme/leaderboard', [[728, 90], [970, 90], [970, 250]], 'div-gpt-ad-leaderboard-0')
        .defineSizeMapping(leaderboardMapping)
        .addService(googletag.pubads())
        // .setTargeting('abtest', [abTestLeaderboardPosition ? 'leaderboard-below-nav': 'leaderboard-above-nav'])
        .setCollapseEmptyDiv(true, true);

      googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-leaderboard-0');

      amsSlots.push({
        slotID: 'div-gpt-ad-leaderboard-0',
        slotName: '/21758830223/nme/leaderboard',
        sizes: [[728, 90], [970, 90], [970, 250]],
      });
    } else {
      // Leaderboard Mobile
      googletag
        .defineSlot('/21758830223/nme/leaderboard', [[300, 50], [320, 50]], 'div-gpt-ad-leaderboard-1')
        .addService(googletag.pubads());

      googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-leaderboard-1');

      amsSlots.push({
        slotID: 'div-gpt-ad-leaderboard-1',
        slotName: '/21758830223/nme/leaderboard',
        sizes: [[300, 50], [320, 50]],
      });
    }

    // Remove sidebar on posts and categories
    if (document.documentElement.clientWidth < 768 && Boolean(wordpress.postId || wordpress.categories)) {
      var sidebarAdSlot = document.querySelector('div[id^="div-gpt-ad-sidebar"]');
      if (sidebarAdSlot) {
        var sidebarElem = sidebarAdSlot.closest('.tdc-column.td-pb-span4');
        if (sidebarElem) {
          sidebarElem.remove();
        }
      }
    }

    for (var sidebarAdsCount = 1; sidebarAdsCount <= 6; sidebarAdsCount++) {
      if (document.getElementById('div-gpt-ad-sidebar-' + sidebarAdsCount)) {
        googletag.defineSlot('/21758830223/nme/mpu', [[300, 600], [300, 250]], 'div-gpt-ad-sidebar-' + sidebarAdsCount)
          .defineSizeMapping(sidebarMapping)
          .addService(googletag.pubads())
          .setTargeting('slot', ['sidebar' + sidebarAdsCount])
          .setCollapseEmptyDiv(true, true);

        googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-sidebar-' + sidebarAdsCount);

        amsSlots.push({
          slotID: 'div-gpt-ad-sidebar-' + sidebarAdsCount,
          slotName: '/21758830223/nme/mpu',
          sizes: [[300, 600], [300, 250]],
        });
      }
    }

    if (document.documentElement.clientWidth < 768) {
      var loopItems = document.querySelectorAll('.tdb-category-loop-posts .tdb_module_loop')
      for (var postsLoopAdsCount = 1; postsLoopAdsCount <= 2; postsLoopAdsCount++) {
        var position = postsLoopAdsCount === 1 ? 2 : 5;
        if (loopItems.length && loopItems[position]) {
          var adElem = document.createElement('div');
          adElem.className = 'tdb_module_loop td_module_wrap td-animation-stack';
          adElem.innerHTML = '<div class="td-a-ad" style="margin-top: 0 !important;">' +
            '<span class="td-adspot-title">Advertisement</span>' +
            '<div id="div-gpt-ad-loop-' + postsLoopAdsCount + '" style="text-align: center;"></div></div>';
          loopItems[position].parentNode.insertBefore(adElem, loopItems[position].nextSibling);

          googletag.defineSlot('/21758830223/nme/mpu', [[300, 250]], 'div-gpt-ad-loop-' + postsLoopAdsCount)
            .addService(googletag.pubads())
            .setTargeting('slot', ['loop' + postsLoopAdsCount])
            .setCollapseEmptyDiv(true, true);

          googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-loop-' + postsLoopAdsCount);

          amsSlots.push({
            slotID: 'div-gpt-ad-loop-' + postsLoopAdsCount,
            slotName: '/21758830223/nme/mpu',
            sizes: [[300, 250]],
          });
        }
      }
    }

    for (var storyAdsCount = 1; storyAdsCount <= 6; storyAdsCount++) {
      if (document.getElementById('div-gpt-ad-story-' + storyAdsCount)) {
        googletag.defineSlot('/21758830223/nme/mpu', [[300, 250], [468, 60], [728, 90], [970, 90], [970, 250]], 'div-gpt-ad-story-' + storyAdsCount)

          slotName: '/21758830223/nme/mpu',
          sizes: [[300, 250], [468, 60], [728, 90], [970, 90], [970, 250]],
        });
      }
    }

    if (wordpress.hidePostAds) {
      return;
    }

      if (document.getElementById('div-gpt-ad-article-' + articleAdsCount)) {
        googletag.defineSlot('/21758830223/nme/mpu', [[300, 250]], 'div-gpt-ad-article-' + articleAdsCount)

        });

      .addService(googletag.pubads());
  });

  <script>
   (function trackImages404s() {
    function requestImage(imageSrc) {
      var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
      xhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
        if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 404) {
          __gaTracker('send', 'event', 'error', 'load-image', imageSrc);
        }
      };
      xhr.open('GET', imageSrc, true);
      xhr.send();
    }

    var elems = document.querySelectorAll('img');
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(elems, function(elem) {
      elem.addEventListener('error', function(event) {
        if (event.target.src.match(/\/wp-content\/uploads/)) {
          requestImage(event.target.src);
        }
      });
    });
  })();
  </script>
